2.02 Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</b></span></p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">On November 15, 2024, IT Tech Packaging, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;)
issued a press release announcing its unaudited financial results for the nine and three months ended September 30, 2024. A copy of the
press release making the announcement is attached as Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K and is incorporated herein by reference.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">The information furnished pursuant to this Item&#160;2.02, including
Exhibit 99.1, shall not be deemed as &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended
(the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section, and shall not be incorporated by reference
into any registration statement or other document filed under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended (the &#8220;Securities Act&#8221;),
or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center"><B>IT Tech Packaging Inc. Announces third Quarter
2024 Unaudited Financial Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">BAODING,&nbsp;China,&nbsp;Nov. 15, 2024&nbsp;/PRNewswire/
--&nbsp;IT Tech Packaging Inc. (NYSE American: ITP) (&ldquo;IT Tech Packaging&rdquo; or the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;), a leading manufacturer
and distributor of diversified paper products in North China, today announced its unaudited financial results for the nine and three
months ended September 30, 2024.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: left; text-indent: -0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><I>Revenue</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">For the third quarter of 2024, total revenue increased
by 59.03%, to&nbsp;approximately $25.08 million&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $15.77 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. This
was mainly due to the increase of sales volume of corrugating medium paper (&ldquo;CMP&rdquo;), partially offset by the decrease in average
selling prices (&ldquo;ASP&rdquo;) of CMP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">The following table summarizes revenue, volume and
ASP by product for the third quarter of 2024 and 2023, respectively:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from CMP, including both regular CMP and
light-Weight CMP, increased by 62.38%, to&nbsp;approximately $25.04 million&nbsp;and accounted for 99.85% of total revenue for the third
quarter of 2024, compared to&nbsp;approximately $15.42 million, or 97.79% of total revenue for the same period of last year. The Company
sold 74,884 tonnes of CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$334/tonne during the third quarter of 2024, compared to 44,396&nbsp;tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$347/tonne
in the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Of the total CMP sales, revenue from regular CMP
increased by 74.93%, to&nbsp;approximately $20.91 million for the third quarter of 2024, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $11.95
million for the same period of last year. The Company sold 62,121 tonnesof regular CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$337/tonne during the third quarter
of 2024, compared to 34,186 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$350/tonne for the same period of last year. Revenue from light-weight CMP increased
by 19.16%, to&nbsp;approximately $4.13 million for the third quarter of 2024, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $3.47 million
for the same period of last year. The Company sold 12,763 tonnes of light-weight CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$324/tonne for the third quarter
of 2024, compared to 10,210 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$340/tonne for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from offset printing paper was $nil for the
three months ended September 30, 2024, compared with revenue of $0.07 million for the same period of last year. The Company sold 170 tonnes
of offset printing paper at an ASP of&nbsp;$407/tonne in the third quarter of 2023.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from tissue paper products was $nil for the
third quarter of 2024, compared to $0.26 million for the third quarter of 2023. The Company sold 241 tonnes of tissue paper products at
an ASP of&nbsp;$1,096/tonne during the third quarter of 2023.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from face masks was $nil for the third quarter
of 2024, compared to $0.02 nillion&nbsp;for the same period of last year. The Company sold 507 thousand pieces of face masks during the
third quarter of 2023.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 2; Options: NewSection; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->2<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><I>Gross Profit and Gross Margin</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total cost of sales increased by 45.46%, to&nbsp;approximately
$23.16 million&nbsp;for the third quarter of 2024 from&nbsp;approximately $15.92 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.&nbsp;
This was mainly due to the increase in sales quantity of CMP, partially offset by the decrease of the unit material cost of CMP products.&nbsp;Costs
of sales per tonne for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, and tissue paper products were&nbsp;$311,&nbsp;$300, $nil
and&nbsp;$nil, respectively, for the third quarter of 2024, compared to $325,&nbsp;$365, $377 and&nbsp;$4,143 respectively, for the same
period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total gross profit was&nbsp;approximately $1.92 million&nbsp;for
the third quarter of 2024, compare to the gross loss of&nbsp;approximately $0.15 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year as a result
of factors described above. Overall gross profit margin was 7.64% for the third quarter of 2024, compared to gross loss margin of 0.97%
for the same period of last year. Gross profit(loss) margins for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, tissue paper products
and face mask products were 7.54%, 7.33%, n/a, n/a and n/a, respectively, for the third quarter of 2024, compared to 7.01%, -7.47%, 7.53%,
-278.10% and -15.75%, respectively, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><I>Selling, General and Administrative Expenses</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Selling, general and administrative expenses (&ldquo;SG&amp;A&rdquo;)
increased by 44.83%, to&nbsp;approximately $3.38 million&nbsp;for the third quarter of 2024 from&nbsp;approximately $2.33 million&nbsp;for
the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><I>Loss from Operations</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Loss from operations was&nbsp;approximately $1.46
million&nbsp;for the third quarter of 2024, a decrease of 41.07%, from loss from operations of&nbsp;approximately $2.48 million&nbsp;for
the same period of last year. Operating loss margin was 5.84% for the third quarter of 2024, compared to operating loss margin of 15.75%
for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><I>Net Loss</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Net loss was&nbsp;approximately $1.97 million, or
loss per share of $0.20, for the third quarter of 2024, compared to net loss of&nbsp;approximately $1.98 million, or loss per share of
$0.20, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><I>EBITDA</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">EBITDA was&nbsp;approximately $2.03 million&nbsp;for
the third quarter of 2024, compared to&nbsp;approximately $1.69 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Note 1: Non-GAAP Financial Measures</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">In addition to our U.S. GAAP results, this press
release includes a discussion of EBITDA, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by the Securities and Exchange Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;).
The Company defines EBITDA as net income before interest, income taxes, depreciation and amortization. EBITDA is a key measure used by
management to evaluate our results and make strategic decisions. Management believes this measure is useful to investors because it is
an indicator of operational performance. Because not all companies use identical calculations, the Company&rsquo;s presentation of EBITDA may
not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies, and should not be viewed as an alternative to measures of financial
performance or changes in cash flows calculated in accordance with the U.S. GAAP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"></P>

    <TD STYLE="border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid; text-align: left">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid; text-align: right">(0.59</TD><TD STYLE="border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid; text-align: left">)</TD><TD STYLE="padding-bottom: 1.5pt">&nbsp;</TD>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><I>Revenue</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">For the nine months ended September 30, 2024, total
revenue decreased by 11.26%, to&nbsp;approximately $58.20 million&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $65.58 million&nbsp;for the same period
of last year. This was mainly due to the decrease in ASP of CMP, partially offset by the increase in sales quantity of regular CMP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">The following table summarizes revenue, volume and
ASP by product for the nine months ended September 30, 2024 and 2023, respectively:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from CMP, including both regular CMP and
light-Weight CMP, decreased by 5.44%, to&nbsp;approximately $58.08 million&nbsp;and accounted for 99.81% of total revenue for the nine
months ended September 30, 2024, compared to&nbsp;approximately $61.43 million, or 93.66% of total revenue for the same period of last
year. The Company sold 168,919 tonnes of CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$344/tonne in nine months ended September 30, 2024, compared to 167,018&nbsp;tonnes
at an ASP of&nbsp;$368/tonne in the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Of the total CMP sales, revenue from regular CMP
decreased by 3.39%, to&nbsp;approximately $48.64 million for the nine months ended September 30, 2024, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately
$50.35 million for the same period of last year. The Company sold 140,574 tonnesof regular CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$346/tonne during the
nine months ended September 30, 2024, compared to 135,912 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$370/tonne for the same period of last year. Revenue
from light-weight CMP decreased by 14.76%, to&nbsp;approximately $9.44 million for the nine months ended September 30, 2023, compared
to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $11.07 million for the same period of last year. The Company sold 28,345 tonnes of light-weight CMP at
an ASP of&nbsp;$333/tonne during the nine months ended September 30, 2023, compared to 31,106 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$356/tonne for
the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from offset printing paper was $nil&nbsp;for
the nine months ended September 30, 2024, compared to $3.23 million for the same period of last year. The Company sold 5,573tonnes of
offset printing paper at an ASP of&nbsp;$579/tonne in the nine months ended September 30, 2023.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from tissue paper products was $nil&nbsp;for
the nine months ended September 30, 2024, compared to $0.83million for the same period of last year. The Company sold 726 tonnes of tissue
paper products at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,145/tonne during the nine months ended September 30, 2023.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from face masks was $nil for the nine months
ended September 30, 2024, compared to $0.10 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. The Company sold 3,023 thousand pieces of face
masks during the nine months ended September 30, 2023.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 5; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->5<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><I>Gross Profit and Gross Margin</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total cost of sales decreased by 18.85%, to&nbsp;approximately
$52.61 million&nbsp;for the nine months ended September 30, 2024 from&nbsp;approximately $64.83 million&nbsp;for the same period of last
year. This was mainly due to the decrease in the unit material costs of CMP. &nbsp;Costs of sales per tonne for regular CMP, light-weight
CMP, offset printing paper, and tissue paper products were&nbsp;$313,&nbsp;$302, n/a and&nbsp;n/a, respectively, for the nine months ended
September 30, 2024, compared to $351,&nbsp;$350, $564 and&nbsp;$4,107, respectively, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total gross profit was&nbsp;approximately $5.58 million&nbsp;for
the nine months ended September 30, 2024, compare to the gross profit of&nbsp;approximately $0.75 million&nbsp;for the same period of
last year as a result of factors described above. Overall gross margin was 9.59% for the nine months ended September 30, 2024, compared
to 1.14% for the same period of last year. Gross profit(loss) margins for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, tissue
paper products and face mask products were 9.44%, 9.33%, n/a, n/a and n/a, respectively, for the nine months ended September 30, 2024,
compared to 5.26%, 1.68%, 2.53%, -258.64% and -9.26%, respectively, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><I>Selling, General and Administrative Expenses</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Selling, general and administrative expenses (&ldquo;SG&amp;A&rdquo;)
increased by 62.51%, to&nbsp;approximately $10.00 million&nbsp;for the nine months ended September 30, 2024 from&nbsp;approximately $6.15
million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><I>Loss from Operations</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Loss from operations was&nbsp;approximately $4.42
million&nbsp;for the nine months ended September 30, 2024, a decrease of 23.50%, from loss from operations of&nbsp;approximately $5.78
million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. Operating loss margin was 7.59% for the nine months ended September 30, 2024, compared
to operating loss margin of 8.81% for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><I>Net Loss</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Net loss was&nbsp;approximately $5.80 million, or
loss per share of $0.58, for the nine months ended September 30, 2024, compared to net loss of&nbsp;approximately $5.96 million, or loss
per share of $0.59, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><I>EBITDA</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">EBITDA was&nbsp;approximately $5.94 million&nbsp;for
the nine months ended September 30, 2024, compared to&nbsp;approximately $5.73 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Note 1: Non-GAAP Financial Measures</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">In addition to our U.S. GAAP results, this press
release includes a discussion of EBITDA, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by the Securities and Exchange Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;).
The Company defines EBITDA as net income before interest, income taxes, depreciation and amortization. EBITDA is a key measure used by
management to evaluate our results and make strategic decisions. Management believes this measure is useful to investors because it is
an indicator of operational performance. Because not all companies use identical calculations, the Company&rsquo;s presentation of EBITDA may
not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies, and should not be viewed as an alternative to measures of financial
performance or changes in cash flows calculated in accordance with the U.S. GAAP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Cash, Liquidity and Financial Position</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">As of September 30, 2024, the Company had cash and
bank balances, short-term debt (including bank loans, current portion of long-term loans from credit union and related party loans), and
long-term debt (including related party loans) of&nbsp;approximately $4.41million,&nbsp;$5.95million and&nbsp;$4.57 million, respectively,
compared to approximately $3.92million,&nbsp;$8.03million and&nbsp;$4.50 million, respectively, as of&nbsp;December 31, 2023.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Net accounts receivable was&nbsp;approximately $1.73&nbsp;million
as of September 30, 2024, compared to $0.58 million as of&nbsp;December 31, 2023. Net inventory was approximately&nbsp;$5.73&nbsp;million
as of September 30, 2024, compared to&nbsp;approximately $3.56&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;December 31, 2023. As of September 30, 2023, the
Company had current assets of&nbsp;approximately $32.97&nbsp;million and current liabilities of&nbsp;approximately$20.75 million, resulting
in a working capital of&nbsp;approximately $12.22&nbsp;million. This was compared to current assets of approximately $28.36 million and
current liabilities of approximately $21.42 million, resulting in a working capital of approximately $6.94 million as of&nbsp;December
31, 2023.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Net cash provided by operating activities was&nbsp;approximately

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><B>About IT Tech Packaging, Inc.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Founded in 1996, IT Tech Packaging, Inc. is a leading
manufacturer and distributor of diversified paper products and single-use face masks in&nbsp;North China. Using recycled paper as its
primary raw material (with the exception of its tissue paper products), ITP produces and distributes three categories of paper products:
corrugating medium paper, offset printing paper and tissue paper products. With production based in Baoding and Xingtai in&nbsp;North
China&rsquo;s&nbsp;Hebei Province, ITP is located strategically close to the&nbsp;Beijing&nbsp;and&nbsp;Tianjin&nbsp;region, home to a growing
base of industrial and manufacturing activities and one of the largest markets for paper products consumption in the country. ITP has
been listed on the NYSE American since&nbsp;December 2009. For more information, please visit:&nbsp;<U STYLE="text-decoration: none">http://www.itpackaging.cn/</U>.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>
